#SHX annexing by CHI
country_event = {
	id = kmt.1
	title = kmt.1.t
	desc = kmt.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					divisions_in_state = { state = 608 size > 15}
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					divisions_in_state = { state = 614 size > 15}
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					divisions_in_state = { state = 607 size > 15}
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = PRC
				factor = -100
			}
		}
		name = kmt.1.a
		CHI = { 
			annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes } 
			country_event = { id = kmt.2 } 
			set_country_flag = shx_sumitted
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Yan Xishan"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					retire_country_leader = yes
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 15 }
		name = kmt.1.b
		CHI = { country_event = { id = kmt.3 days = 1 }}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
		name = kmt.1.c
		effect_tooltip = {
			CHI = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = SHX
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					is_puppet_of = FROM
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				end_puppet = ROOT
			}
		}
		CHI = { country_event = { id = kmt.4 days = 1 }}
		CHI = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = SHX modifier = KMT_SHX_refused }}
		PRC = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = SHX modifier = PRC_SHX_refused }}
		SHX = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = SHX_SHX_refused }}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = refused_shx_offer
		}
	}
}

#declare internal war propaganda lost
country_event = {
	id = kmt.6 
	title = kmt.6.t
	desc = kmt.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	
	fire_only_once = yes
		
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_idea = KMT_propaganda
		OR = {
			has_offensive_war_with = PRC
			has_offensive_war_with = SHX
			has_offensive_war_with = GXC
			has_offensive_war_with = XSM
			has_offensive_war_with = YUN
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }
	
	immediate = {
		CHI = { 
			remove_ideas = KMT_propaganda
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = KMT_propaganda_busted
				days = 600
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.6.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			remove_ideas = KMT_propaganda 
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = KMT_propaganda_busted
				days = 600
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

		}
	}

}

#taiwan refused
country_event = {
	id = kmt.17
	title = kmt.17.t
	desc = kmt.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.17.a
		create_wargoal = {
			type = take_state_focus
			target = FROM
			generator = { 524 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					ROOT = {
						is_faction_leader = no
					}
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				remove_from_faction = ROOT
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							ROOT = {
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
					remove_from_faction = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = kmt.18
	title = kmt.18.t
	desc = kmt.18.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_defensive_war_with = JAP
	}	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.18.a
		add_political_power = 25
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_idea = CHI_nine_power_treaty
							NOT = { tag = CHI }
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = kmt.19 days = 1 }
			}
			USA = { country_event = { id = kmt.19 days = 1 } }
			ENG = { country_event = { id = kmt.19 days = 1 } }
			FRA = { country_event = { id = kmt.19 days = 1 } }
			HOL = { country_event = { id = kmt.19 days = 1 } }
			ITA = { country_event = { id = kmt.19 days = 1 } }
			POR = { country_event = { id = kmt.19 days = 1 } }
			BEL = { country_event = { id = kmt.19 days = 1 } }
			JAP = { country_event = { id = kmt.19 days = 1 } }
			GER = { country_event = { id = kmt.19 days = 1 } }

		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = kmt.19
	title = kmt.19.t
	desc = kmt.19.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_europe_pact
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#maybe we will get help?

		name = kmt.19.a
		trigger = {
			has_idea = CHI_nine_power_treaty
			NOT = { tag = CHI }
		}
		add_political_power = 5
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
	}
	option = {

			tag = JAP

		}

			target = CHI
			modifier = chinese_relations
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = JAP
			}

		}

	}
	#let's attend
	option = {
		name = kmt.19.c
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
			tag = ENG
			tag = FRA
			tag = HOL
			tag = ITA
			tag = POR
			tag = BEL
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CHI
			modifier = chinese_relations
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = JAP
			}
			add_war_support = -0.10
		}	
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 100 
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = JAP
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#Not going
	option = {
		name = kmt.19.e
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
			tag = ENG
			tag = FRA
			tag = HOL
			tag = ITA
			tag = POR
			tag = BEL
		}

			target = CHI
			modifier = western_betrayal
		}

	#Not going JAP

		name = kmt.19.f
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05	
		set_country_flag = no_confrence
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	#Not going GER

			tag = GER
		}

			target = JAP

#CHI wants to join allied
country_event = {
	id = kmt.21
	title = kmt.21.t
	desc = kmt.21.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_europe_pact

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.21.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			create_faction = Allies
		}
		add_to_faction = FROM
		set_global_flag = KMT_eng_accepts_chi_into_faction
		FROM = { country_event = { id = kmt.22} }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.21.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		FROM = { 
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = CHI_join_britain_rejected
			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.23 }
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			id = "CHI"
			type = alliance
			value = -200
		}
	}
}

#baihua stage 1
country_event = {
	id = kmt.33
	title = kmt.33.t
	desc = kmt.33.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politicians_captured
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.34 days = 70 }
		}
	}	

	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		name = kmt.33.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = baihua_end_now
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = conservatism
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = KMT_baihua_stage_1_finished
			days = 365
		}
		set_country_flag = baihua_completed
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = kmt.33.b
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = KMT_baihua_stage_1_idea
			add_idea = KMT_baihua_stage_2_idea
		}
	}
}

#great leap furnace auto build
country_event = {
	id = kmt.40
	title = kmt.40.t
	desc = kmt.40.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_burma_road
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_country_flag = KMT_great_leap_started
		NOT = { has_country_flag = KMT_fully_shitty_furnaced }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 50
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PRC
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
					}
				}
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 1
				}
				save_event_target_as = shitty_furnace_state
			}
		}
	}
				
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.40.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			event_target:shitty_furnace_state = {
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:shitty_furnace_state = {
				set_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
			}
		}
	}
}
		


country_event = {
	id = kmt.41
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_country_flag = KMT_great_leap_started
		NOT = { has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = PRC.owned_states #core_states for PRC is huge
						
						is_core_of = PRC
						#is_owned_by = PRC
						NOT = {
							has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = KMT_fully_shitty_furnaced
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = PRC.owned_states #core_states for PRC is huge
						
					is_core_of = PRC
					#is_owned_by = PRC
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = KMT_fully_shitty_furnaced
		}
	}
	
	option = {}
}

#famine
country_event = {
	id = kmt.43
	title = kmt.43.t
	desc = kmt.43.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop
		}
		has_country_flag = commune_visited
		#any_state = {
		#	has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
		#}
		any_of_scopes = {
			array = Root.controlled_states
			
			has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
				}
				add_manpower = -100000
				set_state_flag = KMT_great_leap_famine
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 
						has_idea = KMT_great_leap_famine_idea 
						has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop
					}
				}
				add_ideas = KMT_great_leap_famine_idea
			}
			add_manpower = -100000
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.43.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = { 
					has_state_flag = KMT_great_leap_famine			
				}
				add_manpower = -100000
			}
			add_manpower = -100000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					has_idea = KMT_great_leap_famine_idea
					has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop	
				}
			}
			add_ideas = KMT_great_leap_famine_idea
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.44 }
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
}

		}

		trigger = {
			tag = ITA

			limit = {
				not = {
					has_global_flag = failed_confrence
				}

			}
		}

		}

				garrison = { x = 0 y = 1 }

#ask sov to integrate sik
country_event = {
	id = kmt.84
	title = kmt.84.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = KMT_sik_refused_demand
			}
		}
		text = kmt.84.d_1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = KMT_sik_refused_demand
		}
		text = kmt.84.d_2
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_japanese_pact
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #declare war
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		name = kmt.84.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = KMT_sik_refused_demand
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -50
			else = {
				add_political_power = 50
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = SIK
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	
	option = { #send demand first
		name = kmt.84.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = KMT_sik_refused_demand
			}
		}
		SIK = { country_event = { id = kmt.483 }}
	}
	
	option = { #send request faction leader help
		name = kmt.84.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			any_allied_country = {
				NOT = {
					tag = ROOT
					tag = SIK
				}
				is_in_faction_with = SIK
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				is_in_faction_with = SIK
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.485 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #send demand first
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		name = kmt.84.e
		add_political_power = -500
		add_stability = -0.2
		SIK = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
				remove_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.118
	title = kmt.118.t
	desc = kmt.118.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_journalists_speech
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	
	##coup
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			728 = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = kmt.118.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = kmt_fascism_tp_728_coup_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = staging_coup_in_728
			728 = {
				owner = {
					country_event = { id = kmt.119 days = 14 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	##gzw for friendship
	option = {
		trigger = {
			728 = {
				owner = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
		}
		name = kmt.118.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		728 = {
			owner = {
				country_event = {
					id = kmt.122 hours = 8
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	##demand
	option = {
		name = kmt.118.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		728 = {
			owner = {
				country_event = { id = kmt.123 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	##occupy
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = KMT_militarism_focus
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		name = kmt.118.e
		custom_effect_tooltip = kmt_fascism_tp_728_inc_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			728 = {
				owner = {
					country_event = { id = kmt.124 }
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 728
			load_oob = "CHI_gzw_occupy"
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.179
	title = kmt.179.t
	desc = kmt.179.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_british_artillery
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = kmt179_triggered
		}
		has_country_flag = incom_indus_ready
		has_tech = basic_machine_tools
		OR = {
			has_tech = concentrated_industry
			has_tech = dispersed_industry
		}
		has_tech = construction1
		OR = {
			AND = {
				num_of_factories > 50
				has_war = no
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_factories > 65
				has_defensive_war = yes
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_factories > 75
				has_offensive_war = yes
			}
		}
		has_idea = incompetent_industry_real
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.179.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = kmt_incompetent_indus_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = incompetent_industry_real
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = incompetent_industry_real
				add_idea = incompetent_industry_real_2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = incompetent_industry_real_navy
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = incompetent_industry_real_navy
				add_idea = incompetent_industry_real_2_navy
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					controller = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = kmt179_triggered
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = KMT_camco_assembly_plants_1
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = KMT_camco_assembly_plants_1
				add_idea = KMT_camco_assembly_plants_2
			}
		}
	}
}

				has_defensive_war = yes
			}

				has_offensive_war = yes

			has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_4 
			has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_5 
			has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_6
			has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_7
			has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_9
			has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_10
		}

					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				}

				}
				remove_ideas = incompetent_industry_real_navy
				remove_ideas = incompetent_industry_fake_navy
				remove_ideas = incompetent_industry_real_2_navy
				remove_ideas = incompetent_industry_real_3_navy
				remove_ideas = incompetent_industry_real_4_navy
				remove_ideas = incompetent_industry_real_5_navy
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = KMT_camco_assembly_plants_1
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_camco_assembly_plants_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = KMT_camco_assembly_plants_2
			}

		}

#enemy close
country_event = {
	id = kmt.203
	title = kmt.203.t
	desc = kmt.203.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_transport_soldiers
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = await_decision_tr 
			has_country_flag = treasures_abroad 
			has_country_flag = treasure_ransacked 
			has_country_flag = no_transfer_tr 
		}
		event_target:KMT_treasure_state = {
			OR = {
				any_neighbor_state = {
					controller = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							tag = JAP
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				controller = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					OR = {
						tag = JAP
						is_puppet_of = JAP
					}
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = await_decision_tr
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.203.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:KMT_treasure_state = {
					controller = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							tag = JAP
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = kmt_national_treasure_ransacked
				days = 900
			}
			set_country_flag = treasure_ransacked
			else = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = kmt_defend_the_treasures
					days = 365
				}
				set_country_flag = no_transfer_tr
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = await_decision_tr
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.203.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:KMT_treasure_state = { state = 613 }
			}
			clear_global_event_target = KMT_treasure_state
			605 = {
				save_global_event_target_as = KMT_treasure_state
				custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_will_be_destination_tt
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:KMT_treasure_state = { state = 605 }
					}
					clear_global_event_target = KMT_treasure_state
					325 = {
						save_global_event_target_as = KMT_treasure_state
						custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_will_be_destination_tt
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								event_target:KMT_treasure_state = { state = 325 }
							}
							clear_global_event_target = KMT_treasure_state
							add_timed_idea = {
								idea = KMT_treasure_abroad_idea
								days = 365
							}
							set_country_flag = treasures_abroad
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = await_decision_tr
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.213

	desc = kmt.213.d

		hidden_effect = {
			white_peace = PRC
			PRC = {
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = joined_kmt_against_prc
					}
					white_peace = PRC
				}
			}
			#every_country = {	
			#	limit = {
			#		has_country_flag = joined_kmt_against_prc
			#	}
			#	white_peace = PRC
			#}

				limit = {
					OR = {

							region = 165
							state = 524
							OR = {
								state = 765
								state = 600
								state = 595
								state = 596
								state = 749
								state = 613
								state = 613
							}
						}
						state = 764
					}
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CHI
						owner = {
							is_puppet_of = CHI
						}
					}
				}
				PRC = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						region = 165
						region = 164

					}

						state = 620
						state = 606

					}

					is_core_of = CHI

				}

	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI

			#any_state = {
			#	NOT = {
			#		state = 524
			#	}
			#	is_owned_by = CHI
			#	is_controlled_by = CHI
			#}
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = owned_states
				
				NOT = { state = 524 }
				is_controlled_by = CHI 
			}
		}
		has_full_control_of_state = 524
		has_war_with = PRC
		NOT = { has_global_flag = status_quo_fired }
		NOT = {
			#any_country = {
			#	OR = {
			#		has_country_flag = joined_kmt_against_prc
			#		has_war_together_with = CHI
			#	}
			#	has_war_with = PRC
			#	has_capitulated = no
			#	exists = yes
			#}
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = PRC.enemies
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = joined_kmt_against_prc
					has_war_together_with = CHI
				}
				has_capitulated = no
				exists = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_controlled_states < 2
				524 = {
					owner = { tag = CHI }
					controller = { tag = CHI }
				}
			}
			PRC = {
				country_event = { id = kmt.217 days = 15 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {}
}

#status quo force peace
country_event = {
	id = kmt.217
	title = kmt.217.t
	desc = kmt.217.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		CHI = {
			has_idea = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
			NOT = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_core_of = CHI
					NOT = {
						state = 524
					}
					#is_owned_by = CHI
					is_controlled_by = CHI
				}
			}
			has_full_control_of_state = 524
			has_war_with = PRC
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = joined_kmt_against_prc
						has_war_together_with = CHI
					}
					has_war_with = PRC
					has_capitulated = no
					exists = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = status_quo_fired
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 95
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_with_major = yes
				factor = 1.25
			}
		}
		name = kmt.217.a
		white_peace = CHI
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					owner =  { tag = CHI }
					NOT = {
						state = 524
					}
				}
				PRC = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = joined_kmt_against_prc
						has_war_together_with = CHI
					}
					has_war_with = PRC
					has_capitulated = yes
					NOT = { tag = XSM }
				}
				PRC = {
					annex_country = {
						target = PREV
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					CHI = {
						has_completed_focus = KMT_north_west_insurgence
					}
				}
				XSM = {
					create_faction = "north_west_insurgence"
					hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = kmt.395 hours = 1 }}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							XSM = {
								has_country_flag = joined_kmt_against_prc
							}
						}
						annex_country = {
							target = XSM
							transfer_troops = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					KOR = { is_puppet_of = CHI }
				}
				puppet = KOR
				KOR = {
					country_event = { id = wd.1 }
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_puppet_of = CHI
				}
				country_event = { id = wd.1 }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = CHI
					is_core_of = PRC
				}
				add_core_of = CHI
				remove_claim_by = CHI
			}
			CHI = {
				remove_ideas = PRC_land_reform_stimulated_our_farmers
				remove_ideas = KMT_harsh_takeover
				remove_ideas = KMT_purge_collaborators
				remove_ideas = KMT_chinese_matter
				remove_ideas = KMT_focus_on_own_army
				remove_ideas = KMT_collaborate_with_collaborators
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
					}
					remove_ideas = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = TWKMT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					TIB = {
						is_in_faction_with = CHI
						has_war_with = PRC
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
				}
				PRC = {
					annex_country = {
						target = TIB
					}
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = kmt_planning_the_civil_war
		}
		set_global_flag = KMT_retreated_to_taiwan
		set_global_flag = forced_ggnz_peace
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		CHI = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.386 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.217.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_with_major = yes
				factor = 0.1
			}
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = PRC_take_taiwan
			days = 400
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			bonus = 0.25
			uses = 4
			category = naval_equipment
			category = air_equipment
			category = marine_tech
			category = para_tech
		}
	}
}

							type = bunker
							level = 1
							province = 1004
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					770 = {
						controller = { 
							OR = {
								tag = CHI 
								is_puppet_of = CHI
							}
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_fortify_land_sd_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					770 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = bunker
							level = 1
							province = 12069
							instant_build = yes
						}
						add_building_construction = {
							type = bunker
							level = 1
							province = 10072
							instant_build = yes
						}
						add_building_construction = {
							type = bunker
							level = 2
							province = 1069
							instant_build = yes
						}
						add_building_construction = {
							type = bunker
							level = 1
							province = 10102
							instant_build = yes
						}
						add_building_construction = {
							type = bunker
							level = 1
							province = 4089
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							770 = {
								owner = { tag = SDC }
							}
						}
						SDC = {
							country_event = { id = kmt.351 } 
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = KMT_faster_fortification
					days = 240
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
			}
		}

			factor = 80
		}
		set_global_flag = KMT_jap_accepts_chi_into_faction
	}

			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = cg_warlords

					has_idea = cg_communist_resistence

				}

		}

			}

				add_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime
			}
		}

				has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_lesser
			}

			}
		}
	}
}

#neutrality election
country_event = {
	id = kmt.279
	title = kmt.279.t
	desc = kmt.279.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KMT_party_chosen
		}
	}
	
	#choose Chiang
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = cks_killed_xian
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		name = kmt.279.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = KMT_implement_parliamentary_system
				}
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = core_states
					
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government
					has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_lesser
					has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime
					has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime_lesser
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 150
			else = {
				add_political_power = 300
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = conservatism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = conservatism
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = nationalism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = despotism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KMT_party_chosen
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.279.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				factor = 120
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Li Zongren"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					army_experience = 50
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.05
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_country_leader = {
									name = "Feng Yuxiang"
									ruling_only = yes
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = {
										has_government = conservatism
									}
									conservatism > 0.6
								}
								set_politics = {
									ruling_party = conservatism
									elections_allowed = yes
								}
								set_party_name = { ideology = conservatism long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
							}
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = conservatism
								popularity = 0.1
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_government = conservatism
								}
								create_country_leader = {
									name = "Feng Yuxiang"
									picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Feng_Yuxiang.dds"
									desc = "POLITICS_FENG_YUXIANG_DESC"
									expire = "1965.1.1"
									ideology = nationalism
									traits = {
										#
									}
								}
							}
							else = {
								add_political_power = -50
								add_popularity = {
									ideology = conservatism
									popularity = -0.05
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		set_country_flag = KMT_party_chosen
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.279.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = conservatism
				}
				conservatism > 0.6
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = conservatism
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = conservatism long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = conservatism
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = cks_killed_xian
				factor = 50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = conservatism
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Ju Zheng"
				desc = "POLITICS_JU_ZHENG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Ju_Zheng.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = nationalism
				traits = {
					KMT_dislike_communism
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Ju Zheng"
				desc = "POLITICS_JU_ZHENG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Ju_Zheng.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = oligarchism
				traits = {
					KMT_dislike_communism
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KMT_party_chosen
	}
}

#YUT dead
country_event = {
	id = kmt.281
	title = kmt.281.t
	desc = kmt.281.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_02
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		YUT = {
			exists = no
		}
		CHI = { 
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = yut_sumitted
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KMT_red_coup_finish
			has_country_flag = KMT_pro_japanese_coup
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = kmt.78.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = jyut_generals_defected
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = cjt_vs_yhm
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = kmt_yhm_join
			set_country_flag = kmt_yhm_flag
			hidden_effect = {
				YUT = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_unit_leader = 1013 }
						remove_unit_leader = 1013
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Yu Hanmou"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
						retire_country_leader = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Chen Jitang"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
						retire_country_leader = yes
					}
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = kmt_cjt_join
				set_country_flag = kmt_cjt_flag
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			YUT = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
			}
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		name = kmt.78.b
		add_stability = 0.01
		add_political_power = 100
	}
}

#reform the army
country_event = {
	id = kmt.285
	title = kmt.285.t
	desc = kmt.285.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	
	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = CHI
		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_weak_army
			has_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
			has_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
		}
		has_army_experience > 349
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = KMT_weak_army
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = KMT_weak_army
					add_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
						}
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
							add_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
								}
								remove_ideas = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			army_experience = -500
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.285.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
					add_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
						}
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = KMT_weak_army
							add_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
						}
						else = {
							remove_ideas = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
						}
					}
				}
			}
			army_experience = -500
		}
	}

			has_government = communism
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = kmt.301.d_2
		trigger = { 
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = PRC_civil_war_started
		OR = {
			tag = SHX
			tag = YUN
			tag = YUT
			tag = GXC
			tag = XSM
			tag = SDC
			tag = SCC
			tag = XIA
			tag = QIA
			tag = ZXL
			tag = SKC
		}
		CHI = {
			has_war_with = PRC
			is_puppet = no
		}
		PRC = {
			is_puppet = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KMT_PRC_joined
		}
		CHI = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = KMT_pro_japanese_coup
				has_country_flag = KMT_red_coup_finish
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = KMT_PRC_joined
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.301.a

			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = CHI
				enemy = PRC
			}
			set_country_flag = joined_kmt_against_prc

				country_event = { id = kmt.302 }
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
			else = {
				PRC = {
					country_event = { id = kmt.302 }
					annex_country = {
						target = ROOT
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.301.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

#scorch earth
country_event = {
	id = kmt.328
	title = kmt.328.t
	desc = kmt.328.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #disabled atm, wasnt triggered only 
	
	trigger = {
		always = no #is_triggered_only = yes 
		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in_1
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in_2
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in_3
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in_4
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			controller = {
				has_offensive_war_with = ROOT
			}
			NOT = {
				has_state_flag = scorched
			}
		}
	}
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					controller = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = scorched
					}
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 4
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						PREV = {
							arms_factory > 0
						}
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
					}
					set_state_flag = scorch_removed_af_tt
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								PREV = {
									industrial_complex > 0
								}
							}
							remove_building = {
								type = industrial_complex
								level = 1
							}
							set_state_flag = scorch_removed_ic_tt
						}
					}
				}
				set_state_flag = scorched
				set_state_flag = scorched_tt
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.328.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorched_tt
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 4
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorch_removed_af_tt
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorch_removed_ic_tt
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorched_tt
				}
				clr_state_flag = scorched_tt
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorch_removed_ic_tt
				}
				clr_state_flag = scorch_removed_ic_tt
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorch_removed_af_tt
				}
				clr_state_flag = scorch_removed_af_tt
			}
		}
	}
}

				has_country_flag = CQ_send_troops
			}
			add_manpower = -100
			army_experience = 1
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				remove_from_faction = FROM
				FROM = {
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_war_together_with = ROOT
							}
							country_event = { id = wd.1 }
						}
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = FROM
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_war_together_with = ROOT
							}
							country_event = { id = wd.1 }
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = ROOT
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = kmt.343.t
	desc = {
		text = kmt.344.d_stall
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				has_country_flag = KMT_stall_time
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = kmt.344.d_c
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = KMT_seek_cob
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		name = kmt.343.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_CQ_stall_time_tt
		set_country_flag = PRC_stall_time
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 9
		}
		name = kmt.344.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			FROM = {
				remove_from_faction = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_together_with = FROM
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = wd.1 }
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.345 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		name = kmt.344.b
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = KMT_seek_cob
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				PRC = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				CHI = { remove_ideas = KMT_chinese_matter }
				PRC = { remove_ideas = kmt_planning_the_civil_war }
			}
			FROM = {
				create_faction = KMT_united_chinese_gov
				add_to_faction = ROOT
				add_ai_strategy = {
					id = "PRC"
					type = alliance
					value = 200
				}
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					annex_country = {
						target = ROOT
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.346 hours = 2 }
		}
	}
}

#retreat to taiwan
country_event = {
	id = kmt.347
	title = kmt.347.t
	desc = kmt.347.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_full_control_of_state = 524
		tag = CHI
		PRC = { 
			has_war_with = ROOT 
			is_puppet = no
		}
		OR = {
			num_of_controlled_states < 4
			surrender_progress > 0.79
		}
		has_global_flag = PRC_restart_chinese_civil_war
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 } 
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 100 
			modifier = {
				factor = 80
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
		}
		name = kmt.347.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = ROOT
				NOT = {
					state = 524
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			remove_core_of = ROOT
		}
		add_ideas = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
		set_capital = 524
		add_political_power = -50
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0 
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
		}
		name = kmt.347.b
	}
}

#chi abandon us
country_event = {
	id = kmt.349
	title = kmt.349.t
	desc =  kmt.349.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_transport_soldiers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PGR
			}
			clr_global_flag = PGR_wait_bridge
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SDC
			}
			clr_global_flag = SDC_wait_bridge
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				tag = SDC
				factor = 1
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = bridge_choose_die
		JAP = { 
			country_event = { id = kmt.350 }
			puppet = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PGR
				country_exists = EHA
				EHA = { is_puppet_of = JAP }
			}
			EHA = {
				country_event = { id = jap.4 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PGR
			}
			add_state_claim = 615
			add_state_claim = 770
			add_state_claim = 614
			add_state_claim = 597
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1050 } remove_unit_leader = 1050 }
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1051 } remove_unit_leader = 1051 }
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1052 } remove_unit_leader = 1052 }
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1053 } remove_unit_leader = 1053 }
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1054 } remove_unit_leader = 1054 }
		}
		name = kmt.349.a
	}
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PGR
			}
			clr_global_flag = PGR_wait_bridge
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SDC
			}
			clr_global_flag = SDC_wait_bridge
		}
		set_global_flag = MP_bridge_resisted
		name = kmt.349.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				tag = SDC
				factor = 99
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = bridge_choose_def
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_puppet_of = CHI
			}
			CHI = {
				end_puppet = ROOT
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.350 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = chose_defy_jap
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

						}

							is_puppet_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					MEN = {
						transfer_state = 611
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						has_country_flag = bridge_choose_def
					}
				}

					target = FROM
					type = puppet_wargoal_focus
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.361
	title = kmt.361.t
	desc = kmt.361.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_defensive_war_with = JAP
		USA = {
			has_completed_focus = USA_limited_intervention
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.320.a
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = 10000 producer = USA }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_1 amount = 200 producer = USA }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = light_tank_equipment_1 amount = 100 producer = USA }
		if = {
			limit = { USA = { has_tech = tech_curtiss_p40_equipment_1 } }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = curtiss_p40_equipment_1 amount = 300 producer = USA }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { USA = { has_tech = tech_curtiss_p36_equipment_1 } }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = curtiss_p36_equipment_1 amount = 300 producer = USA }
		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = usa_boeing_p26_equipment_2 amount = 300 producer = USA }
		}
	}
}

#border war lost
country_event = {
	id = kmt.362
	title = kmt.362.t
	desc = kmt.362.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			owns_state = 752
			owns_state = 622
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		752 = {
			set_border_war = no
		}
		622 = {
			set_border_war = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 752
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							NOT = { state = 752 }
							#is_owned_by = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				622 = {
					owner = {
						annex_country = {
							target = ROOT
							transfer_troops = no
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					622 = {
						owner = {
							transfer_state = 752
						}
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				622 = {
					owner = {
						country_event = { id = kmt.363 }
						set_country_flag = bdw_622
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 622
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							NOT = { state = 622 }
							#is_owned_by = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				752 = {
					owner = {
						annex_country = {
							target = ROOT
							transfer_troops = no
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					752 = {
						owner = {
							transfer_state = 622
						}
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				752 = {
					owner = {
						country_event = { id = kmt.363 }
						set_country_flag = bdw_752
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.362.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 752
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							any_owned_state = {
								NOT = { state = 752 }
								#is_owned_by = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					622 = {
						owner = {
							annex_country = {
								target = ROOT
								transfer_troops = no
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						622 = {
							owner = {
								transfer_state = 752
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 622
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							any_owned_state = {
								NOT = { state = 622 }
								#is_owned_by = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					752 = {
						owner = {
							annex_country = {
								target = ROOT
								transfer_troops = no
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						752 = {
							owner = {
								transfer_state = 622
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.367
	title = kmt.367.t
	desc = kmt.367.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_02
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = JAP
		}
		has_global_flag = CHI_warred_with_JAP
		is_puppet = no
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_global_flag = KMT_purge_collaborators_flag
		name = kmt.367.a
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = KMT_purge_collaborators
			days = 365
		}
		PRC = {
			country_event = {
				id = kmt.368 hours = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 89
		}
		name = kmt.367.b
		add_political_power = 200
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = KMT_harsh_takeover
			days = 600
		}
			if = {
				limit = {
					MEN = {
						has_tech = infantry_weapons
						NOT = {
							has_tech = infantry_weapons1
						}
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_0 amount = 2500 producer = MEN }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					MAN = {
						has_tech = infantry_weapons
						NOT = {
							has_tech = infantry_weapons1
						}
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_0 amount = 2500 producer = MAN }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					JAP = {

	id = kmt.386
	title = kmt.386.t
	desc = kmt.386.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.386.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			white_peace = PRC
		}
	}
}

#power struggle
country_event = {
	id = kmt.387
	title = kmt.387.t
	desc = kmt.387.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_01
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Li Zongren"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_country_flag = cks_retire
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = KMT_li_chiang_rivalry
			set_global_flag = kmt387_fired
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.387.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_ideas = KMT_li_chiang_rivalry
		}
	}
}

#power struggle
country_event = {
	id = kmt.388
	title = kmt.387.t
	desc = kmt.388.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_01
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Li Zongren"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_country_flag = cks_retire
		has_global_flag = kmt387_fired
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = kmt.388.a
		retire_country_leader = yes
		if = {
			limit ={
				has_government = conservatism
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = nationalism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = despotism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_unit_leader = 1010
			}
			remove_unit_leader = 1010
		}
		remove_ideas = KMT_li_chiang_rivalry
		add_political_power = -200
		set_country_flag = KMT_li_left
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		name = kmt.388.b
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = KMT_li_chiang_rivalry
			add_idea = KMT_li_chiang_rivalry_2
		}
	}
}

#return indochina?
country_event = {
	id = kmt.389
	title = kmt.389.t
	desc = kmt.389.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_01
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_war_with = JAP
		671 = {
			controller = {
				has_war_together_with = ROOT
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			is_owned_by = JAP
		}
		670 = {
			controller = {
				has_war_together_with = ROOT
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			is_owned_by = JAP
		}
		741 = {
			controller = {
				has_war_together_with = ROOT
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			is_owned_by = JAP
		}
		286 = {
			controller = {
				has_war_together_with = ROOT
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			is_owned_by = JAP
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	#back to france
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FRA
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		name = kmt.389.c
		FRA = {
			transfer_state = 671
			transfer_state = 670
			transfer_state = 741
			transfer_state = 286
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_returned_indochina
			}
			give_military_access = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	#nothing
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 8 }
		name = kmt.389.e
	}
}

#chi civil war
country_event = {
	id = kmt.392
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = CHI
		has_idea = cg_true
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = KMT_special_japan16_civil_war
			has_civil_war = yes
		}
		any_country = {
			original_tag = CHI
			NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			NOT = {
				OR = { 
					AND = { 
						has_government = neutrality
						ROOT = { has_government = neutrality }
					}
					AND = { 
						has_government = conservatism
						ROOT = { has_government = conservatism }
					}
					AND = { 
						has_government = communism
						ROOT = { has_government = communism }
					}
					AND = { 
						has_government = fascism
						ROOT = { has_government = fascism }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = kmt392_fired
				has_global_flag = xian_civil_war
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = kmt392_fired
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = PRC
					has_idea = cg_warlords
				}
				is_puppet = no
				has_civil_war = no
			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.393 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
	}
}

#chi civil war
country_event = {
	id = kmt.393
	title = kmt.393.t
	desc = kmt.393.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_01
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = PRC
			has_idea = cg_warlords
		}
		is_puppet = no
		has_civil_war = no
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				any_allied_country = {
					original_tag = CHI
					has_civil_war = yes
				}
				any_country = {
					original_tag = CHI
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_war_together_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 49
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				has_government = fascism
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				has_government = neutrality
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				has_government = communism
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_government = conservatism
				}
				has_government = conservatism
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Wang Jingwei"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				add = -500
			}
		}
		name = kmt.393.a
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CHI
				has_civil_war = yes
				has_war_with = FROM
				NOT = {
					tag = FROM
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = FROM
					enemy = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 49
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					any_enemy_country = {
						original_tag = CHI
						has_civil_war = yes
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					any_enemy_country = {
						original_tag = CHI
						has_civil_war = yes
						has_government = ROOT
					}
				}
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				any_country = {
					NOT = {	tag = FROM }
					original_tag = CHI
					has_war_with = FROM
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Wang Jingwei"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				add = -500
			}
		}
		name = kmt.393.b
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CHI
				has_civil_war = yes
				has_war_with = FROM
				NOT = {
					tag = FROM
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = PREV
					enemy = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.393.c
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CHI
				has_civil_war = yes
				has_war_with = FROM
				NOT = {
					tag = FROM
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.393.e
	}
}

	}

#neutrality election
country_event = {
	id = kmt.397
	title = kmt.279.t
	desc = kmt.397.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = KMT_party_chosen
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KMT_second_election_passed
		}
	}
	
	#choose Chiang
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = cks_killed_xian
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_global_flag = KMT_chiang_dead
			}
		}
		name = kmt.279.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = conservatism
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = nationalism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = despotism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KMT_second_election_passed
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.279.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				factor = 120
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Li Zongren"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					army_experience = 50
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.05
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_country_leader = {
									name = "Feng Yuxiang"
									ruling_only = yes
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = {
										has_government = conservatism
									}
									conservatism > 0.6
								}
								set_politics = {
									ruling_party = conservatism
									elections_allowed = yes
								}
								set_party_name = { ideology = conservatism long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
							}
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = conservatism
								popularity = 0.1
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_government = conservatism
								}
								create_country_leader = {
									name = "Feng Yuxiang"
									picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Feng_Yuxiang.dds"
									desc = "POLITICS_FENG_YUXIANG_DESC"
									expire = "1965.1.1"
									ideology = nationalism
									traits = {
										#
									}
								}
							}
							else = {
								if = {
									limit = {
										has_country_leader = {
											name = "Ju Zheng"
											ruling_only = yes
										}
									}
									add_popularity = {
										ideology = conservatism
										popularity = -0.03
									}
									add_popularity = {
										ideology = communism
										popularity = -0.05
									}
									else = {
										add_political_power = -50
										add_popularity = {
											ideology = conservatism
											popularity = -0.05
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KMT_second_election_passed
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.397.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = conservatism
				}
				conservatism > 0.6
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = conservatism
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = conservatism long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = conservatism
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = cks_killed_xian
				factor = 50
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KMT_second_election_passed
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = conservatism				
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Xu Fulin"
				desc = "POLITICS_XU_FULIN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/Asia/Portrait_Asia_Generic_2.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = nationalism
				traits = {
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Xu Fulin"
				desc = "POLITICS_XU_FULIN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/Asia/Portrait_Asia_Generic_2.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = oligarchism
				traits = {
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

			add_political_power = 15

				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.1
			}

#elections
country_event = {
	id = kmt.401
	title = kmt.279.t
	desc = kmt.397.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Yen Chia-kan"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			has_government = conservatism
		}
		has_country_flag = KMT_second_election_passed
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = cks_killed_xian
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		name = kmt.279.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = conservatism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = conservatism
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = nationalism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = despotism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.279.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Li Zongren"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			army_experience = 50
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Feng Yuxiang"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_government = conservatism
							}
							conservatism > 0.6
						}
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = conservatism
							elections_allowed = yes
						}
						set_party_name = { ideology = conservatism long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = conservatism
						popularity = 0.1
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = conservatism
						}
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Feng Yuxiang"
							picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Feng_Yuxiang.dds"
							desc = "POLITICS_FENG_YUXIANG_DESC"
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = nationalism
							traits = {
								#
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_country_leader = {
									name = "Ju Zheng"
									ruling_only = yes
								}
							}
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = conservatism
								popularity = -0.03
							}
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = communism
								popularity = -0.05
							}
							else = {
								add_political_power = -50
								add_popularity = {
									ideology = conservatism
									popularity = -0.05
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.401.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = conservatism
				}
				conservatism > 0.6
			}
			set_politics = {	
				ruling_party = conservatism
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = conservatism long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = conservatism
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		retire_country_leader = yes
	}
}

#sino soviet neutrality
country_event = {
	id = kmt.407
	title = kmt.407.t
	desc = kmt.407.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_idea = KMT_SOV_JAP_neutrality
				JAP = {
					has_war_with = CHI
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment_1 > 8000 }
			has_equipment = { support_equipment > 2500 }
		}
		name = kmt.407.a
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = CHI
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = KMT_SOV_neutrality_pact }
		CHI = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = SOV
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { modifier = KMT_SOV_neutrality_pact target = SOV }
			country_event = { id = kmt.408 }
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = 8000
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = support_equipment
			amount = 2500
		}
		set_global_flag = KMT_sino_soviet_neutrality
		add_ideas = KMT_assistance_to_CHI
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.407.b
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				has_global_flag = KMT_german_approved_global
				OR = {
					GER = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_government = neutrality
								same_ideo_with_ROOT = yes
								is_in_faction_with = ROOT
								is_puppet_of = ROOT
								has_war_together_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					has_opinion = {
						target = GER
						value < -44
					}
				}
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				has_global_flag = KMT_JAP_agreed_to_assist
				OR = {
					JAP = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_government = neutrality
								same_ideo_with_ROOT = yes
								is_in_faction_with = ROOT
								is_puppet_of = ROOT
								has_war_together_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					has_opinion = {
						target = JAP
						value < -44
					}
				}
				add = 100
			}
		}
		CHI = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.409 }
		}
		add_ideas = KMT_assistance_to_CHI
	}
}

#bandits
country_event = {
	id = kmt.415
	title = kmt.415.t
	desc = kmt.415.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	
	trigger = {
		has_idea = KMT_PRC_bandits
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = KMT_PRC_bandits_cooldown
				days > 30
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = KMT_PRC_bandits_cooldown
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 25 }
	
	immediate = { 
		clr_country_flag = KMT_PRC_bandits_cooldown
		set_country_flag = KMT_PRC_bandits_cooldown
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.414.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					
					any_neighbor_state = {
						controller = {
							has_idea = KMT_PRC_bandits
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						controller = {
							has_idea = KMT_PRC_bandits
						}
					}
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 4
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						industrial_complex > 0
					}
					damage_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						damage = 1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					damage_building = {
						type = infrastructure
						damage = 4
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							industrial_complex > 0
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = industrial_complex
							damage = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.422
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_chinese_nations = yes
		owns_state = 728
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = KMT_use_postal_romanisation
			}	
			728 = { set_state_name = KMT_postal_STATE_728_returned }
			else = {
				728 = { set_state_name = KMT_STATE_728_returned }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.423
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = KMT_check_non_ai_chinese_player_flag
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = {
				flag = KMT_check_non_ai_chinese_player_flag
				value = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			modify_global_flag = {
				flag = KMT_check_non_ai_chinese_player_flag
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.424
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = {
					flag = KMT_check_non_ai_chinese_player_flag
					value < 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						is_chinese_nations = yes
						NOT = { tag = SIK }
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						is_chinese_nations = yes
						NOT = { tag = SIK }
						is_ai = no
					}
					country_event = { id = kmt.420 }
				}
				else = {
					CHI = { country_event = { id = kmt.420 }}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.424.a
	}
}

#XIA dead
country_event = {
	id = kmt.426
	title = kmt.426.t
	desc = kmt.426.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_02
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		XIA = {
			exists = no
		}
		CHI = { 
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = xia_sumitted
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KMT_red_coup_finish
			has_country_flag = KMT_pro_japanese_coup
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = JAP
				factor = 100
			}
		}
		name = kmt.426.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = kmt_xia_generals_join
		set_country_flag = kmt_tsz_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			XIA = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "He Jian"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					retire_country_leader = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Cheng Qian"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					retire_country_leader = yes
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
			}
			CHI = {
				set_country_flag = xia_sumitted
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = JAP
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = kmt.426.b
		add_stability = 0.01
		add_political_power = 100
	}
}

#aaa
country_event = {
	id = kmt.430
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			WJW = {
				is_puppet_of = JAP
				exists = yes
			}
			CHI = {
				OR = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
				exists = yes
			}
			HYQ = {
				OR = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
				exists = yes
			}
			any_country = {
				is_chinese_nations = yes
				is_puppet_of = JAP
				exists = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				WJW = {
					exists = yes
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = JAP
						is_in_faction_with = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_chinese_nations = yes
						tag = HYQ
					}
					exists = yes
					NOT = { tag = SIK }
					is_puppet_of = JAP
					NOT = { tag = WJW }
				}
				WJW = {
					annex_country = {
						target = PREV
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						HYQ = {
							exists = yes
							OR = {
								is_puppet_of = JAP
								is_in_faction_with = JAP
							}
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_chinese_nations = yes
								tag = WJW
							}
							exists = yes
							NOT = { tag = SIK }
							is_puppet_of = JAP
							NOT = { tag = HYQ }
						}
						HYQ = {
							annex_country = {
								target = PREV
								transfer_troops = no
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								CHI = {
									exists = yes
									OR = {
										is_puppet_of = JAP
										is_in_faction_with = JAP
									}
								}
							}
							every_country = {
								limit = {
									OR = {
										is_chinese_nations = yes
										tag = WJW
										tag = HYQ
									}
									exists = yes
									NOT = { tag = SIK }
									is_puppet_of = JAP
									NOT = { tag = CHI }
								}
								CHI = {
									annex_country = {
										target = PREV
										transfer_troops = no
									}
								}
							}
							else = {
								random_country = {
									limit = {
										is_chinese_nations = yes
										is_subject_of = JAP
									}
									save_event_target_as = KMT_JAP_temp_annex_actor
								}
								every_country = {
									limit = {
										is_chinese_nations = yes
										exists = yes
										NOT = { tag = SIK }
										is_puppet_of = JAP
										NOT = { tag = CHI }
									}
									event_target:KMT_JAP_temp_annex_actor = {
										annex_country = {
											target = PREV
											transfer_troops = no
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {}
}

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CHI
				NOT = { tag = CHI }
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
			ROOT = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_popularities = {
			conservatism = 5
			fascism = 5
			communism = 1
			neutrality = 89
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = {
					flag = KMT_pro_jap_action_count
					value > 0
				}
				has_global_flag = {
					flag = KMT_pro_jap_action_count
					value < 3
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Feng Yuxiang"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Feng_Yuxiang.dds"
				desc = "POLITICS_FENG_YUXIANG_DESC"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = oligarchism
				traits = {
					#
				}
			}
			else = {				
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
					desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC_DESC"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = despotism
					traits = {
						KMT_cks_generallissimo
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {}
}

#warlord faction
country_event = {
	id = kmt.435
	title = kmt.435.t
	desc = kmt.435.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politicians_captured
	
	trigger = {
		always = no
		CHI = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = KMT_warlord_after_civil_war
				has_completed_focus = KMT_warlord
			}
			has_war_with = ROOT
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = cg_warlords
			has_idea = cg_warlords_ssc
			has_idea = cg_displaced_warlords
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = pending_warlord_faction_event	
			has_country_flag = dont_want_be_warlord_faction_leader	
			has_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader	
			any_country = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = cg_warlords
					has_idea = cg_warlords_ssc
					has_idea = cg_displaced_warlords
				}
				OR = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					has_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
				}
				has_war_with = CHI
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			CHI = { 
				OR = {
					has_wargoal_against = PREV 
					has_war_with = PREV
				}
			}
			
			OR = {
				has_idea = cg_warlords
				has_idea = cg_warlords_ssc
				has_idea = cg_displaced_warlords
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = pending_warlord_faction_event
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = kmt.434.a
		create_faction = "anti_alliance"
		set_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
		clr_global_flag = pending_warlord_faction_event
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.434.a
		set_country_flag = dont_want_be_warlord_faction_leader
		clr_global_flag = pending_warlord_faction_event
	}
}

#warlord faction
country_event = {
	id = kmt.436
	title = kmt.435.t
	desc = kmt.435.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politicians_captured
	
	trigger = {
		always = no
		CHI = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = KMT_warlord_after_civil_war
				has_completed_focus = KMT_warlord
			}
			has_war_with = ROOT
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = cg_warlords
			has_idea = cg_warlords_ssc
			has_idea = cg_displaced_warlords
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = dont_want_be_warlord_faction_leader
		}
		any_country = {
			NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			CHI = { 
				OR = {
					has_wargoal_against = PREV 
					has_war_with = PREV
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				has_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
			}
			OR = {
				has_idea = cg_warlords
				has_idea = cg_warlords_ssc
				has_idea = cg_displaced_warlords
			}
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = kmt.434.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					has_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
				}
				create_faction = "anti_alliance"
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
			}
			add_to_faction = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.434.a
		set_country_flag = dont_want_be_warlord_faction_leader
	}
}

#the hump
country_event = {
	id = kmt.507
	title = kmt.507.t
	desc =  kmt.507.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_airplane_factory
	
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = CHI
		}
		exists = yes
		has_capitulated = no
		is_puppet = no
		is_alone_or_in_faction_at_peace_with_CHI = yes
		has_idea = KMT_assistance_to_CHI
		CHI = {
			exists = yes
			is_puppet = no
			has_defensive_war_with = JAP
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = CHI.controlled_states
						
						is_coastal = yes
					}
				}
				surrender_progress > 0.24
				AND = {
					613 = {
						controller = { has_war_with = CHI }
					}
					608 = {
						controller = { has_war_with = CHI }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			is_puppet_of = JAP
			is_in_faction_with = JAP
			has_non_aggression_pact_with = JAP
			has_war_with = CHI
			is_puppet_of = CHI
		}
		OR = {
			747 = {
				controller = {
					OR = {
						has_war_with = CHI
						has_war_with = ENG
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				640 = {
					controller = {
						OR = {
							has_war_with = CHI
							has_war_with = ENG
						}
					}
				}
				766 = {
					controller = {
						OR = {
							has_war_with = CHI
							has_war_with = ENG
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		432 = {
			controller = { 
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CHI
					has_war_with = USA
				}
			}
		}
		325 = {
			controller = { 
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CHI
					has_war_with = USA
				}
				OR = {
					tag = CHI
					is_in_faction_with = CHI
					is_puppet_of = CHI
					has_war_together_with = CHI
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.507.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_war_with = CHI
					has_opinion = {
						target = CHI
						value < -69
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				432 = {
					controller = {
						is_puppet = yes
					}
				}
			}
			432 = {
				controller = {
					overlord = {
						country_event = { id = kmt.508 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				432 = {
					controller = {
						country_event = { id = kmt.508 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
					}
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			432 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = air_base
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			CHI = {
				add_ideas = KMT_the_hump_idea
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					has_war_with = CHI
					has_opinion = {
						target = CHI
						value < -69
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = kmt.507.b
	}
}
