#from withdraw support
country_event = {
	id = kmt.538
	title = kmt.538.t
	desc = kmt.538.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_army_mountainside
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = ENG }
				OR = {
					has_idea = KMT_burma_road_idea
					has_idea = KMT_burma_road_idea_closed
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_burma_road_idea
			remove_ideas = KMT_burma_road_idea_closed
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = FRA }
				OR = {
					has_idea = KMT_yunnan_bahn_idea
					has_idea = KMT_yunnan_bahn_idea_closed
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_yunnan_bahn_idea
			remove_ideas = KMT_yunnan_bahn_idea_closed
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = USA }
				OR = {
					has_idea = KMT_ledo_road_idea
					has_idea = KMT_ledo_road_idea_closed
					has_idea = KMT_the_hump_idea
					has_idea = KMT_the_hump_idea_closed
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_ledo_road_idea
			remove_ideas = KMT_ledo_road_idea_closed
			remove_ideas = KMT_the_hump_idea
			remove_ideas = KMT_the_hump_idea_closed
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = GER }
				OR = {
					has_idea = german_advisors
					has_idea = KMT_sino_german_joint_research
					has_idea = KMT_sino_german_joint_research_ger_adv
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = german_advisors
			remove_ideas = KMT_sino_german_joint_research
			remove_ideas = KMT_sino_german_joint_research_ger_adv
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = sino_german_cooperation
				target = GER
			}
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = more_sino_german_coop_trade
				target = GER
			}
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = more_sino_german_coop
				target = GER
			}
			GER = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = sino_german_cooperation
					target = CHI
				}
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = more_sino_german_coop_trade
					target = CHI
				}
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = more_sino_german_coop
					target = CHI
				}
			}
			if = {

#communist revolution!
country_event = {
	id = kmt.539
	title = kmt.539.t
	desc = kmt.539.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_riot
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.539.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				is_subject_of = CHI
				CHI = { has_government = communism }
				factor = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = fascism
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = yes
				NOT = { is_subject_of = CHI }
			}
			overlord = { 
				remove_from_faction = ROOT
				end_puppet = ROOT 
				country_event = { id = kmt.544 }
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = communism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.5
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = -1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = conservatism
			popularity = -0.25
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = KMT_communists_overthrow_white_peace_window_flag
			activate_mission = KMT_communists_overthrow_white_peace_window_mission
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.539.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_capital = no
					#is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = communism
				size = 0.5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = CHI
				}
				CHI = { 
					end_puppet = ROOT 
					random_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = ROOT
							has_government = communism
						}
						CHI = {
							puppet = PREV
						}
						declare_war_on = {
							target = ROOT
							type = annex_everything
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				CHI = {
					create_wargoal = {
						target = ROOT
						type = puppet_wargoal_focus
					}
					country_event = { id = kmt.543 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = kmt.566.t
	desc = kmt.566.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.566.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ROOT
					type = civil_war
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#relate back to .430
country_event = {
	id = kmt.567
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_event_target = KMT_first_chinese_puppet_of_jap }
		OR = {
			WJW = {
				is_puppet_of = JAP
				exists = yes
			}
			CHI = {
				OR = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
				exists = yes
			}
			HYQ = {
				OR = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
				exists = yes
			}
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.chinese_nations
				
				#is_chinese_nations = yes
				is_puppet_of = JAP
				exists = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	
	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_chinese_nations = yes
							tag = WJW
						}
						is_puppet_of = JAP
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = CHI
							tag = HYQ
						}
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
							is_in_faction_with = JAP
						}
					}
				}
				exists = yes
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = KMT_first_chinese_puppet_of_jap
		}
	}
	
	option = {}
}

#relate back to .430
country_event = {
	id = kmt.568
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_event_target = KMT_first_chinese_puppet_of_jap
		NOT = { country_exists = event_target:KMT_first_chinese_puppet_of_jap }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	
	immediate = {
		clear_global_event_target = KMT_first_chinese_puppet_of_jap
	}
	
	option = {}
}

#relate back to .430
country_event = {
	id = kmt.569
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_event_target = KMT_first_chinese_puppet_of_jap
		any_country = {
			NOT = {
				tag = event_target:KMT_first_chinese_puppet_of_jap
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						is_chinese_nations = yes
						tag = WJW
					}
					is_puppet_of = JAP
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						tag = CHI
						tag = HYQ
					}
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = JAP
						is_in_faction_with = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			exists = yes
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	
	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.430 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {}
}

country_event = { #Soviet Air Purchase Y1
	id = kmt.600
	title = kmt.600.t
	desc = kmt.600.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_meeting
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.600.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			has_equipment = { fighter_equipment > 150 }
			has_equipment = { light_bomber_equipment > 75 }
			is_ai = no
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = fighter_equipment
			amount = 150
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = light_bomber_equipment
			amount = 75
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.601 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.600.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			has_equipment = { fighter_equipment > 150 }
			is_ai = no
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = fighter_equipment
			amount = 150
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.602 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.600.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.603 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.600.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = yes
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = i_15_equipment_1 amount = 150 producer = SOV }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = sb_2m_bomber_equipment_1 amount = 75 producer = SOV }
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = i_15_equipment_1
			amount = 150
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = sb_2m_bomber_equipment_1
			amount = 75
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.601 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.600.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SOV_CHI_air_purchase_1_delay }
		}
		FROM = {
			SOV = { 
				country_event = { id = kmt.600 days = 30 }
				set_country_flag = SOV_CHI_air_purchase_1_delay
			}
		}
	}
	
	
}

country_event = { #Soviet Air Purchase Y2
	id = kmt.604
	title = kmt.604.t
	desc = kmt.604.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_meeting
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.604.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			has_equipment = { fighter_equipment > 200 }
			has_equipment = { light_bomber_equipment > 100 }
			is_ai = no
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = fighter_equipment
			amount = 200
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = light_bomber_equipment
			amount = 100
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.605 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.604.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			has_equipment = { fighter_equipment > 200 }
			is_ai = no
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = fighter_equipment
			amount = 200
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.606 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.604.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.607 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.604.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { has_tech = tech_i_16_equipment_3 } }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = i_16_equipment_3 amount = 100 producer = SOV }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = i_15_equipment_2 amount = 100 producer = SOV }
			send_equipment = {
				target = CHI
				type = i_16_equipment_3
				amount = 100
			}
			send_equipment = {
				target = CHI
				type = i_15_equipment_2
				amount = 100
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = i_15_equipment_2 amount = 200 producer = SOV }
			send_equipment = {
				target = CHI
				type = i_15_equipment_2
				amount = 200
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = sb_2m_bomber_equipment_1 amount = 100 producer = SOV }
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = sb_2m_bomber_equipment_1
			amount = 100
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.605 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.604.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SOV_CHI_air_purchase_2_delay }
		}
		FROM = {
			SOV = { 
				country_event = { id = kmt.604 days = 30 }
				set_country_flag = SOV_CHI_air_purchase_2_delay
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Soviet Air Purchase Y3
	id = kmt.608
	title = kmt.608.t
	desc = kmt.608.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_meeting
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.608.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			has_equipment = { fighter_equipment > 250 }
			has_equipment = { light_bomber_equipment > 125 }
			is_ai = no
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = fighter_equipment
			amount = 250
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = light_bomber_equipment
			amount = 125
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.609 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.608.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			has_equipment = { fighter_equipment > 250 }
			is_ai = no
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = fighter_equipment
			amount = 250
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.610 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.608.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.611 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.608.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { has_tech = tech_i_153_equipment_1 } }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = i_153_equipment_1 amount = 150 producer = SOV }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = tech_i_16_equipment_3 amount = 100 producer = SOV }
			send_equipment = {
				target = CHI
				type = i_153_equipment_1
				amount = 150
			}
			send_equipment = {
				target = CHI
				type = tech_i_16_equipment_3
				amount = 100
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = tech_i_16_equipment_3 amount = 250 producer = SOV }
			send_equipment = {
				target = CHI
				type = tech_i_16_equipment_3
				amount = 250
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = sb_2m_bomber_equipment_1 amount = 125 producer = SOV }
		send_equipment = {
			target = CHI
			type = sb_2m_bomber_equipment_1
			amount = 125
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.609 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kmt.608.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SOV_CHI_air_purchase_3_delay }
		}
		FROM = {
			SOV = { 
				country_event = { id = kmt.608 days = 30 }
				set_country_flag = SOV_CHI_air_purchase_3_delay
			}
		}
	}
}
